
The parity check matrix for W(3,25) minus a spread is a 26b x 
25b matrix, where b is 626.

The 1 coordinates of the first row of the circulants in the (q+1)xq rep matrix is \
given by Hrep.

The length of the code is 15650 and the check matrix has rank 
8451, so the full code has dimension 7199.

There is a generator matrix for the subcode of the form (P | id) where P is quasi \
cyclic 11b x 14b matrix, whose first rows are in the matrix Pbin.

The subcode has dimension 6886 so the rate is 0.44.
